The window of the room faces the sea view. When I get up in the morning, I can see the sun rising. The scenery is very beautiful. The layout of the room is the same as the pictures provided by the hotel. The sun is very sunny during the day, and the sunshine is very sufficient. The outdoor swimming pool is very large and clean, but the indoor swimming pool is temporarily closed. We saw weddings in the hotel for two days, both indoors and outdoors. The hotel has a large lawn and a camping place. I brought my children to play, one big and two small. The room is standardly equipped with only one set of children's supplies, but after communicating with the hotel's room service, the hotel will replenish the children's daily necessities. I especially like the children's bathrobes provided by the hotel. They are very nice. If there are problems with the cleaning of the room, I will communicate with the room service staff and deal with it quickly. The hotel breakfast variety is not too much, enough for the three of us to eat well. I especially recommend the egg omelette for breakfast. Watching the chef cook on the spot, it feels fresher and delicious. Other facilities include a table tennis room and a children's playroom. It is recommended to add foam splicing cushions to the bottom of the ocean pool in the children's playroom. When my child jumped down from the low slope, his feet became red and swollen because the ground was made of hard plastic mats. I told the hotel sister at the door about the situation and she helped to spray Yunnan Baiyao. The first aid kit is still standard. There are also some self-funded projects, such as children's painting and fishing. I rented a 30-minute double bicycle to go around the hotel. I can also go out of the hotel and ride along the beach. When I stepped on the beach behind the Tianhou Temple, there was no road, so I stepped back. It was exactly 30 minutes.
In general, the experience is still good. During the National Day, you don't have to squeeze with others outside, nor do you have to get stuck in traffic on the road. The subway can go directly to the hotel entrance, and you can have fun. I will also recommend friends to bring their children here to play, and I will choose this hotel next time.
